Tikapaṭṭhāna, Part II

[page 069]
                               69
                          [KUSALATTIKAṂ
                          PAṬICCAVĀRO
                         A. PAṆṆATTIVĀRO.1
                1. Hetupaccayo. (a) Anulomaṃ.]
     (i) Siyā kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo dhammo
uppajjeyya hetupaccayā?2
     (ii) Siyā kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca akusalo dhammo
uppajjeyya hetupaccayā?
     (iii) Siyā kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca avyākato dhammo
uppajjeyya hetupaccayā?
     Siyā kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca
     (iv) . . . kusalo ca avyākato ca dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā?
     (v) . . . akusalo ca avyākato ca dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā?
     (vi) . . . kusalo ca akusalo ca dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā?
     (vii) . . . kusalo ca akusalo ca avyākato ca dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ
hetupaccayā?
     (viii) Siyā akusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca
          (a) akusalo dhammo, uppajjeyya hetupaccayā?
          (b) kusalo dhammo, uppajjeyya hetupaccayā?
          (c) avyākato dhammo uppajjeyya hetupaccayā?
     Siyā akusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca
          (d) akusalo ca avyākato ca, dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā?
          (e) kusalo ca avyākato ca, dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā?
          (f) kusalo ca akusalo ca, dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā?
          (g) kusalo ca akusalo ca avyākato ca dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā?
     (ix) Siyā avyākataṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca
          (a) avyākato dhammo, uppajjeyya hetupaccayā?
          (b) kusalo dhammo, uppajjeyya hetupaccayā?
          (c) akusalo dhammo, uppajjeyya hetupaccayā?
     Siya avyākataṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca
          (d) kusalo ca avyākato ca, dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā?
          (e) akusalo ca avyākato ca, dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā?
          (f) kusalo ca akusalo ca, dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā?
          (g) kusalo ca akusalo ca avyākato ca dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā?
--------------------------------------------------------------------------
1 Udāhu pañhavāro, udāhu pucchāvāro. Comy.
2 Such of these possible relations as actually occur are answered
affirmatively in the Niddesavāro, p. 73.


[page 070]
70                     Kusalattikaṃ
     (x) Siyā kusalañ ca avyākatañ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca
          (a) kusalo dhammo, uppajjeyya hetupaccayā?
          (b) akusalo dhammo, uppajjeyya hetupaccayā?
          (c) avyākato dhammo, uppajjeyya hetupaccayā?
          (d) kusalo ca avyākato ca dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā?
          (e) akusalo ca avyākato ca dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā?
          (f) kusalo ca akusalo ca dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā?
          (g) kusalo ca akusalo ca avyākatā ca dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā?
     (xi) Siyā akusalañ ca avyākatañ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca
          (a) kusalo dhammo, uppajjeyya hetupaccayā?
          (b) akusalo dhammo, uppajjeyya hetupaccayā?
          (c) avyākato dhammo, uppajjeyya hetupaccayā?
          (d) kusalo ca avyākato ca dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā?
          (e) akusalo ca avyākato ca dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā?
          (f) kusalo ca akusalo ca dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā?
          (g) kusalo ca akusalo ca, avyākato ca dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā?
     Siyā kusalañ ca akusalañ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca
          (a)-(g) as above.
     Siyā kusalañ ca akusalañ ca avyākatañ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca
          (a)-(g) as above.
                               2.
     Siyā kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo dhammo uppajjeyya
ārammaṇapaccayā? . . .
     Yathā hetupaccayo vitthārito. Evaṃ ārammaṇapaccayo
pi vitthāretabbo vācanā maggena . . . evaṃ adhipatipaccayo
. . . avigatapaccayo pi vitthāretabbo vācanā maggena.
                          Ekamūlakaṃ.
     Siyā kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo dhammo uppajjeyya
hetupaccayā ārammaṇapaccayā . . . pe . . . hetupaccayā
avigatapaccayā ?
                          Dumūlakaṃ.
     Siyā kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo dhammo uppajjeyya
hetupaccayā ārammaṇapaccayā adhipatipaccayā . . . pe . . .
hetupaccayā ārammaṇapaccayā avigatapaccayā?
                          Timūlakaṃ.

[page 071]
                          Paṭiccavāro                          71
     Siyā kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo dhammo uppaj-
jeyya hetu,- ārammaṇa-, adhipati-, anantarapaccayā . . .
pe . . . hetu-, ārammaṇa-, adhipati-, avigatapaccayā?
                          Catumūlakaṃ.
     Pañcamūlamūkādikā saṅkhittā. Ekamūlakaṃ, dumūlakaṃ,
ti-, catu-, pañca-, sabbamūlakaṃ asaṃmuyhantena vitthāre-
tabbaṃ.
                          Hetumūlakaṃ.
                               2-24.
     So for the other paccayas (2-24).
     Ekekassa padassa ekamūlakaṃ, dumūlakaṃ, timūlakaṃ,
catumūlakaṃ, pañcamūlakaṃ, sabbamūlakaṃ asaṃmuyhantena
vitthāretabbaṃ.
          Tikañ ca paṭṭhānavaraṃ dukuttamaṃ
          Dukaṃ tikañ ceva tikaṃ dukañ ca
          Tikaṃ tikañ ceva dukaṃ dukañ ca
          Cha anulomamhi nayā sugambhīrā ti.
                         [b. Paccanīyaṃ.]
     Siyā kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo dhammo uppajjeyya
na-hetupaccayā? . . . (Yathā anulome hetupaccayo vitthāre-
tabbo, evaṃ paccanīye pi na-hetupaccayo vitthāretabbo).
     Siyā kusalaṃ dhammaṃ . . . na-ārammaṇapaccayā . . .
na adhipatipaccayā . . . pe . . . no-atthipaccayā . . . no-
natthipaccayā . . . no-vigatapaccayā . . . no avigatapac-
cayā? . . .
     Siyā kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo dhammo uppajjeyya
na-hetupaccayā na-ārammaṇapaccayā? . . . (Yathā anu-
lome ekekassa padassa ekamūlakaṃ, dumūlakaṃ, timūlakaṃ,
catumūlakaṃ, yāva tevīsatimūlaṃ, evaṃ paccanīye pi vitthāre-
tabbaṃ).
     Tikañ ca . . . (here follows the quatrain as above, sub-
stituting cha paccanīyamhi for cha anulomamhi).

[page 072]
72                     Kusalattikaṃ
                     [c. Anulomapaccanīyaṃ.]
     Siyā kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo dhammo uppaj-
jeyya hetupaccayā na-ārammaṇapaccayā . . . akusalo
dhammo uppajjeyya. . . .
     (Yathā anulome hetupaccayo vitthārito, evaṃ anulomapac-
canīye pi padaṃ vitthāretabbaṃ.)
     Siyā kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo dhammo uppajjeyya
hetupaccayā na-adhipatipaccayā? . . . hetupaccayā na-
anantarapaccayā? . . . pe . . . hetupaccayā no-avigatapac-
cayā? . . .
     Siyā kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo dhammo uppaj-
jeyya (a) hetupaccayā ārammaṇapaccayā na-adhipatipac-
cayā? . . . na-anantarapaccayā ? . . . pe . . . no-avigata-
paccayā? . . . (b) hetupaccayā ārammaṇapaccayā adhi-
patipaccayā na-anantarapaccayā ? . . . hetu-, ārammaṇa-
adhipati-paccayā no-avigatapaccayā? . . . pe . . .
     Siyā kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo dhammo uppajjey-
ya ārammaṇapaccayā . . . avigatapaccayā ? . . . na-hetu-
paccayā . . . avigatapaccayā ? . . . na-ārammaṇapaccayā
. . . avigatapaccayā no-vigatapaccayā . . . avigatapaccayā
hetupaccayā na-ārammaṇapaccayā . . . avigatapaccayā?
. . . hetupaccayā no-vigatapaccayā . . . avigatapaccayā ?
. . . hetu- ārammaṇa-paccayā nādhipati-paccayā . . . avi-
gatapaccayā? . . . hetu- ārammaṇa-no-vigata-paccayā . . .
avigatapaccayā ? . . . hetupaccayā ārammaṇapaccayā . . .
pe . . . no-vigatapaccayā? . . .
     Tikañ ca paṭṭhānaṃ . . . pe . . . .1
     Cha anuloma-paccanīyamhi nayā sugambhīrā ti.
                     [Paccanīyānulomaṃ.]
     Siyā kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo dhammo uppajjeyya
na-hetupaccayā ārammaṇapaccayā ? . . . na-hetupaccayā
adhipatipaccayā? . . . pe . . . na-hetupaccayā avigata-
paccayā? . . .
--------------------------------------------------------------------------
1 The quatrain as above save in last line.


[page 073]
                          Paticcavāro                         73
     Siyā kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo dhammo uppajjey-
ya na-hetupaccayā na-ārammaṇapaccayā adhipatipaccayā
. . . pe . . . avigatapaccayā? . . . na-hetupaccayā na-āram-
maṇapaccayā na-adhipatipaccayā . . . pe . . . avigatapac-
cayā? . . . pe . . . no-atthi- . . . no-natthi- . . . novigata-
paccayā avigatapaccayā ? . . .
     Siyā kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo dhammo uppajjeyya
nārammaṇapaccayā1 hetupaccayā ? . . . na-ārammaṇa-
paccayā1 adhipatipaccayā? . . . pe . . . na-ārammaṇa-
paccayā avigatapaccayā? . . . pe . . . no-atthipaccayā
hetupaccayā? . . . no-avigatapaccayā ārammaṇapaccayā?
. . . pe . . . no-avigatapaccayā vigatapaccayā? . . . no-
avigatapaccayā na-hetupaccayā ārammaṇapaccayā? . . .
no-avigatapaccayā na-hetupaccayā vigatapaccayā? . . .
no-avigatapaccayā na-hetupaccayā na-ārammaṇapaccayā na-
adhipatipaccayā?. . . pe . . . no-atthipaccayā no-natthi-
paccayā vigatapaccayā?
     Tikañ ca paṭṭhānaṃ . . . (the quatrain as above but)
     Cha paccanīyānulomamhi nayā sugambhīrā ti
                     Paṇṇattivāro niṭṭhito.
                         [B. NIDDESAVĀRO.]
                          1 (hetu).
     (i)2 Kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo dhammo uppajjati
hetupaccayā.
     Kusalaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā,
          tayo khandhe paṭicca eko khandho,
          dve khandhe paṭicca dve khandhā . . .
     (iii) Kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca avyākato khandho uppajjati
hetupaccayā.
     Kusale khandhe paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ . . .
--------------------------------------------------------------------------
1 B. sic
2 Cf. corresponding questions in Paṇṇattivāro, p. 69 f.


[page 074]
74                          Kusalattikaṃ
     (iv) Kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo ca avyākato ca
dhammā uppajjanti hetupaccayā.
     Kusalaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ,
          tayo khandhe paṭicca eko khandho citta-, etc.
          dve khandhe paṭicca dve khandhā citta-, etc.
     (viii, a) Akusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca akusalo dhammo uppajjati
hetupaccayo.
     Akusalaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ . . . (as above).
     (viii, c) Akusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca avyākato dhammo uppajjati
hetupaccayā.
     Akusale khandhe paṭicca . . . (as above).
     (viii, d) Akusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca akusalo ca avyākato
ca dhammā uppajjanti hetupaccayā.
     Akusalaṃ ekaṃ . . . tayo . . . dve . . . (as above).
     (ix, a) Avyākataṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca avyākato dhammo
uppajjeyya hetupaccayā.
     Vipākavyākataṃ kiriyāvyākataṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ tayo
khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ . . . dve khandhe
paṭicca dve khandhā citta . . . pe . . .
     Paṭisandhikkhaṇe vipākāvyākataṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca
tayo khandhā kaṭattā ca rūpaṃ . . . tayo khandhe paṭicca
eko khandho kaṭattā ca rūpaṃ . . . dve khandhe paṭicca
dve khandhā kaṭattā ca rūpaṃ . . . khandhe paṭicca vatthuṃ
. . . vatthuṃ paṭicca khandhā . . . ekaṃ mahābhūtaṃ paṭicca
tayo mahabhūtā . . . tayo mahābhūte paṭicca ekaṃ ma-
hābhūtaṃ . . . dve mahābhūte paṭicca dve mahābhūtā . . .
mahābhūte paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ . . . kaṭattā-
rūpaṃ upādā-rūpaṃ . . .
     (x, c) Kusalañ ca avyākatañ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca avyākato
dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Kusale khandhe ca mahābhūte ca paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ
rūpaṃ . . .
     (xi, c) Akusalañ ca avyākatañ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca avyākato
dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Akusale khandhe ca mahābhūte ca paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ . . .

[page 075]
                          Paṭiccavāro                     75
                               2.1
     (i) Kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo dhammo uppajjati
ārammaṇapaccayā . . . (continue as in 1).
     (viii, a) Akusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca akusalo dhammo uppajjati
ārammaṇapaccayā (continue as under 1, viii, a).
     (ix, a) Avyākataṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca avyākato dhammo
uppajjati ārammaṇapaccayā.
     Vipākāvyākataṃ kiriyāvyākataṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca
tayo khandhā . . . tayo khandhe paṭicca eko khandho . . .
dve khandhe paṭicca dve khandhā . . .
     Paṭisandhikkhaṇe vipākāvyākataṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca
tayo khandhā . . . tayo khandhe paṭicca eko khandho . . .
dve khandhe paṭicca dve khandhā . . . vatthuṃ paṭicca
khandhā . . .
                               3.
     (i) Kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo dhammo uppajjati
adhipatipaccayā . . . (continue as before).
     (iii) Kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca avyākato dhammo uppajjati
adhipatipaccayā.
     Kusale khandhe paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ . . .
     (iv) Kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo ca avyākato ca
dhammā uppajjanti adhipatipaccayā.
     Kusalaṃ ekaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā cittasamutthānañ ca rūpaṃ . . .
     Kusalaṃ tayo khandhe paṭicca eko khandho cittasamutthānañ ca rūpaṃ . . .
     Kusalaṃ dve khandhe paṭicca dve khandhā cittasamutthānañ ca rūpaṃ . . .
     (viii, a) Akusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca akusalo dhammo
uppajjati adhipatipaccayā.
     . . . ekaṃ . . . tayo . . . tayo . . . ekaṃ . . . dve . . .
dve. . . .
     (viii, c) Akusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca avyākato dhammo
uppajjati adhipatipaccayā.
     Akusale khandhe paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ.
     (viii, d) Akusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca akusalo ca avyākato
ca dhammā uppajjanti adhipatipaccayā.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------
1 Cf. Nos. of paccayas on p. iii.


[page 076]
76                     Kusalattikaṃ
     Akusalaṃ ekaṃ . . . (as above 1, c) . . . cittasamuṭṭhānañ
ca rūpaṃ.
     (ix, a) Avyākataṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca avyākato dhammo
uppajjati adhipaṭipaccayā.
     Vipākāvyākataṃ kiriyāvyākataṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca
tayo khandhā.
          tayo khandhe . . . eko . . . samuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ.
          dve khandhe . . . dve . . . samuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ.
     Ekaṃ mahābhūtaṃ paṭicca tayo mahābhūtā . . .
          tayo mahābhūte paṭicca ekaṃ mahabhūtaṃ . . .
          dve mahābhūte paṭicca dve mahābhūtā . . .
mahābhūte paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ upādā rūpaṃ.
     (x, c) Kusalañ ca avyākatañ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca avyākato
dhammo uppajjati adhipatipaccayā.
     Kusale khandhe ca mahābhūte ca paṭicca cittasamutthānaṃ
rūpaṃ.
     (xi, c) Akusalañ ca avyākatañ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca avyākato
dhammo uppajjati adhipatipaccayā.
     Akusale khandhe ca mahābhūte ca paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ . . .
                               4, 5.
     (i) Kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo dhammo uppajjati
anantara-paccayā . . . samanantarapaccayā.
     Kusalaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā . . .
     Anantaraṃ pi samanantaraṃ pi ārammaṇapaccaya-sadisaṃ.
                               6.
     (i) Kusalaṃ . . . kusalo . . . uppajjati sahajātapaccayā.
     Kusalaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo . . .
          tayo khandhe paṭicca eko . . .
          dve khandhe paṭicca dve . . .
     (iii) Kusalaṃ . . . avyākato . . . uppajjati sahajātapaccayā.
     Kusale khandhe paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ.

84                     Kusalattikaṃ
                         [Gaṇanā-mūlakā.1]
          Hetuyā nava                Kamme nava
          Ārammaṇe tīṇi                Vipāke ekaṃ
          Adhipatiyā nava               Āhāre nava
          Anantare tīṇi                Indriye nava
          Samanantare tīṇi           Jhāne nava
          Sahajāte nava                Magge nava
          Aññamaññe tīṇi                Sampayutte tīṇi
          Nissaye nava                Vippayutte nava
          Upanissaye tīṇi               Atthiyā nava
          Purejāte tīṇi                Natthiyā tīṇi
          Āsevane tīṇi                Vigate tīṇi
                                         Avigate nava.
     Hetupaccayā      [Hetumūlakā.]
          ārammaṇe tīṇi           samanantare tīṇi
          adhipatiyā nava          sahajāte nava
          anantare tīṇi           aññamaññe tīṇi . . .
                                    etc., as in list above.
     Hetupaccayā      [Dumūlakaṃ.]
          ārammaṇapaccayā          anantare tīṇi
          adhipatiyā tīṇi          samanantare tīṇi . . .
                All tīṇi except vipāke ekaṃ.
                          [Timūlakaṃ.]
     Hetupaccayā ārammaṇapaccayā adhipatipaccayā anan-
tara-, samanantara-, sahajāta-, aññamañña-, nissaya-, upanis-
saya-, purejāta-,2 āsevana-paccayā kamme tīṇi . . . avigate
tīṇi (omitting vipāka-).
                          [Sesamūlakā.]
     Hetupaccayā . . . vigatapaccayā avigatapaccayā tīṇi
     Hetupaccayā . . . pe . . . purejāta-, kamma-, vipāka-,
āhāre ekaṃ . . . avigate ekaṃ.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------
1 Cf. Comy. here on.
2 Omitting pacchājāta-.


[page 085]
                          Paṭiccavāro                          85
     Hetupaccayā . . . pe . . . purejātapaccayā kammapac-
cayā . . . vigatapaccayā avigate ekaṃ.
                    Gaṇanā-hetumūlakā niṭṭhitā.
     Ārammaṇe ṭhitena sabbattha tīṇ' eva pañhā.
     Ārammaṇapaccayā hetuyā tīṇi.
                     adhipatiyā tīṇi . . . pe . . .
                     avigate tīṇi.
     Adhipatipaccayā hetuyā nava
                     ārāmmaṇe tīṇi . . . pe . . .
                     avigate nava.
     Anantarapaccayā hetuyā tīṇi . . . pe . . . avigate tīṇi.
     samanantarapaccayā hetuyā tīṇi . . . pe . . . avigate tīṇi.
     Sahajātapaccayā hetuyā nava . . . pe . . .
     Aññamaññapaccayā hetuyā tīni.
     Nissayapaccayā hetuyā nava,
     Upanissayapaccayā hetuyā tīṇi.
     Purejātapaccayā hetuyā tīṇi,
     Āsevanapaccayā hetuyā tīṇi,
                    ārammaṇe tīṇi . . . pe . . .
                    purejāte tīṇi,
                    kamme tīṇi,
                    āhāre tīṇi . . . pe . . .
                    avigate tīṇi.
          Āsevanamūlake vipākaṃ natthi.
     Kammapaccayā hetuyā nava
     Vipākapaccayā hetuyā ekaṃ,
                ārammaṇe ekaṃ . . . pe . . .
                purejāte ekaṃ,
                kamme ekaṃ
                āhāre ekaṃ . . . pe . . .
                avigate ekaṃ.
          Vipākamūlake āsevanaṃ natthi.

[page 086]
86                     Kusalattikaṃ
     Āhārapaccayā hetuyā nava.
     Indiryapaccayā hetuyā nava.
     Jhānapaccayā hetuyā nava.
     Maggapaccayā hetuyā nava.
     Sampayuttapaccayā hetuyā tīṇi,
     Vippayuttapaccayā hetuyā nava,
     Atthipaccayā hetuyā nava,
     Natthipaccayā hetuyā tīṇi
     Vigatapaccayā hetuyā tīṇi
     Avigatapaccayā hetuyā nava,
                    ārammaṇe tīṇi,
                    adhipatiyā nava,
                    natthiyā tīṇi,
                    vigate tīṇi.
     Ekekaṃ paccayaṃ mūlakaṃ kātun asajjhāyantena gaṇetabbā ti.

                     1. Hetu-ekamūlakaṃ.]

na-ārammaṇe pañca (Na-Ā 5) | na-vipāke nava      (Na-V 9)
na-adhipatiyā nava (Na-A 9) | na-indriye ekaṃ     (Na-I 1)
na-anantare pañca (Na-An 5) | na-jhāne ekaṃ      (Na-Jh 1)
na-samanantare pañca (Na-S 5) | na-magge ekaṃ      (Na-M 1)
na-aññamaññe pañca (Na-Añ 5) | na-sampayutte pañca (Na-Sp 5)
na-upanissaye pañca (Na-U 5) | na-vippayutte tīṇi (Na-Vpp 3)
na-purejāte satta (Na-Pu 7) | no-natthiyā pañca (No-Nat 5)
na-pacchājāte nava (Na-Pa 9) | no-vigate pañca     (No-Vg 5)
na-āsevane nava      (Na-Ās 9) |

                         Paccanīyānulomaṃ.
                     Paṭiccavāro niṭṭhito.
                          [Sahajātavāro
                          Anulomaṃ.]
                               1.
     (i) Kusalaṃ dhammaṃ sahajāto kusalo dhammo uppajjati
hetupaccayā.
     Kusalaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ sahajātā tayo khandhā; tayo
khandhe sahajāto eko khandho; dve khandhe sahajātā dve
khandhā.
     (iii) Kusalaṃ dhammaṃ sahajāto avyākato dhammo uppaj-
jati hetupaccayā.
     Kusale khandhe sahajātaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ.
     (iv) Kusalaṃ dhammaṃ sahajāto kusalo ca avyākato ca
dhammā uppajjanti hetupaccayā.
     Kusalaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ. Sahajātā tayo khandhā citta-
samuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ, tayo khandhe sahajāto eko khandho
cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ; dve khandhe sahajātā dve
khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ.
     (viii, a) Akusalaṃ dhammaṃ sahajāto akusalo dhammo
uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Akusalaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ sahajātā tayo khandhā, tayo
. . . eko . . .; dve . . . dve khandhā.
     Akusalaṃ dhammaṃ sahajāto avyākato dhammo uppajjati
hetupaccayā.
     Akusale khandhe sahajātaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ.
     (viii, d) Akusalaṃ dhammaṃ sahajāto akusalo ca avyākato
ca dhammā uppajjanti hetupaccayā.
     Akusalaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ sahajātā tayo khandhā cittasam-
uṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ; tayo . . . eko . . .; dve . . . dve . . .
     (ix, a) Avyākataṃ dhammaṃ sahajāto avyākato dhammo
uppajjati hetupaccayā.

108                     Kusalattikaṃ

tayo khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ tayo . . . eko
. . .; dve . . . dve . . .
     Paṭisandhikkhaṇe vipākāvyākataṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ saha-
jātā tayo khandhā kaṭattā ca rūpaṃ; so for tayo . . .
eko . . .; dve . . . dve . . .
     Khandhe sahajātaṃ vatthu; vatthuṃ sahajātā khandhā.
     Ekaṃ mahābhūtaṃ sahajātā tayo mahābhūtā; so for tayo
. . . ekaṃ . . .; dve . . . dve. . . . Mahābhūte sahajātaṃ
cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ kaṭattārūpaṃ upādārūpaṃ.
     (x, c) Kusalañ ca avyākatañ ca dhammaṃ sahajāto avyākato
dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Kusale khandhe ca mahābhūte ca sahajātaṃ cittasamuṭṭhā-
naṃ rūpaṃ.
     (xi, c) Akusalañ ca avyākatañ ca dhammaṃ sahajāto avyākato
dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Akusale khandhe ca mahābhūte ca sahajātaṃ cittasamuṭ-
ṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ.

     (viii, a) Akusalaṃ dhammaṃ paccayā akusalo dhammo up-

     Akusalaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paccayā tayo khandhā; so for

                          Paccayavāro.
                          [NISSAYAVĀRO
                          Anulomaṃ.]
     (i) Kusalaṃ dhammaṃ nissāya kusalo dhammo uppajjati
hetupaccayā.
     Kusalaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ nissāya tayo khandhā; tayo
khandhe nissāya eko khandho; dve khandhe nissāya dve
khandhā.
     (iii) Kusalaṃ . . . avyākato . . . uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Kusale khandhe nissāya cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ.
     (iv) Kusalaṃ dhammaṃ nissāya kusalo ca avyākato ca
dhamma uppajjanti hetupaccayā.
     Kusalaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ nissāya tayo khandhā cittasamuṭ-
ṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ; tayo . . .; dve . . . cittasamuṭṭhānañ
ca rūpaṃ.
     (viii, a) Akusalaṃ . . . akusalo . . . uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Akusalaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ nissāya tayo khandhā . . . pe
. . . dve khandhe nissāya dve khandhā.
     (viii, c) Akusalaṃ dhammaṃ nissāya avyākato dhammo up-
pajjati hetupaccayā.
     Akusale khandhe nissāya cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ.
     (viii, d) Akusalaṃ dhammaṃ nissāya akusalo ca avyākato
ca dhammā uppajjanti hetupaccayā.
     Akusalaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ nissāya tayo khandhā cittasam-
uṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ . . . pe . . . dve khandhā cittasam-
utthānañ ca rūpaṃ.
     (ix, a) Avyākataṃ dhammaṃ nissāya avyākato dhammo
uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Vipākāvyākataṃ kiriyāvyākataṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ nissāya
tayo khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ . . . pe . . .
dve khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ.
     Paṭisandhikkhane vipākāvyākataṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ nissāya

tayo khandhā kaṭattā ca rūpaṃ, tayo . . . dve khandhi
kaṭattā ca rūpaṃ. Khandhe nissāya vatthu; vatthuṃ nis-

bhūte nissāya ekaṃ mahābhūtaṃ; dve . . . dve mahābhūtā.

pajjati na-hetupaccayā.

nissāya tayo khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ; tayo
khandhe . . . dve khandhe . . .
     Ahetukapaṭisandhikkhaṇe vipākāvyākataṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ
nissāya tayo khandhā kaṭattā ca rūpaṃ . . . dve khandhā
kaṭattā ca rūpaṃ. Khandhe nissāya vatthu; vatthuṃ nissāya
khandhā.
     Ekaṃ mahābhūtaṃ nissāya tayo mahābhūtā, mahābhūte
nissāya cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ kaṭattā rūpaṃ, upādā rūpaṃ.
Bāhiraṃ . . . Āhārasamuṭṭhānaṃ . . . Utusamuṭṭhānaṃ . . .

khandhānaṃ kaṭattā ca rūpānaṃ hetupaccayena paccayo.

     Kusalo . . . kusalassa . . . ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.

taṃ paccavekkhati; pubbe suciṇṇāni paccavekkhati; jhānā

cavekkhanti, vodānaṃ paccavekkhanti; sekhā maggā vuṭ-
ṭhahitvā maggaṃ paccavekkhanti; sekhā vā puthujjanā vā
kusalaṃ aniccato dukkhato anattato vipassanti, cetopari-
yañāṇena kusalacittasamaṅgissa cittaṃ jānanti.
     Ākāsānañcāyatanakusalaṃ viññaṇañcāyatanakusalassa
ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     Ākiñcaññāyatanakusalaṃ nevasaññā-nāsaññāyatanakusa-
lassa ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.

pubbenivāsānussatiñāṇassa yathākammūpagañāṇassa anāga-
taṃsañāṇassa ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.

156                     Kusalattikaṃ
     Akusalā khandhā cetopariyañāṇassa pubbenivāsānussati-
ñaṇassa yathākammūpagañāṇassa anāgataṃsañāṇassa āvaj-
janāya ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     Akusalo . . . avyākatassa . . . ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     Arahā pahīnakilese paccavekkhati, pubbe samudāciṇṇe
kilese jānāti, akusalaṃ aniccato dukkhato anattato vipas-
sati, cetopariyañāṇena akusalacittasamaṅgissa cittaṃ jānāti.
Sekhā vā puthujjanā vā akusalaṃ aniccato dukkhato anattato
vipassanti.
     Akusale niruddhe vipāko tad-ārammaṇatā uppajjati. Aku-
salaṃ assādeti abhinandati; taṃ ārabbha rāgo uppajjati, diṭṭhi
. . . vicikicchā . . . uddhaccaṃ . . . domanassaṃ uppajjati.
Akusale niruddhe vipāko tad-ārammaṇatā uppajjati. Aku-
salā khandhā cetopariyañāṇassa pubbenivāsānussatiñāṇassa
yathākammūpagañāṇassa anāgataṃsañāṇassa āvajjanāya
ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     Avyākato . . . avyākatassa . . . ārammaṇapaccayena pac-
cayo.
     Arahā phalaṃ paccavekkhati, nibbānaṃ paccavekkhati.
Nibbānaṃ phalassa āvajjanāya ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
Arahā cakkhuṃ aniccato dukkhato anattato vipassati, sotaṃ,
ghānaṃ, jivhaṃ, kāyaṃ, rūpe, sadde, gandhe, rase, phoṭṭhabbe,
vatthuṃ . . .
     Vipākāvyākate kiriyāvyākate khandhe aniccato dukkhato
anattato vipassati, dibbena cakkhunā rūpaṃ passati, dibbāya
sotadhātuyā saddaṃ suṇāti, cetopariyañāṇena vipākāvyāka-
takiriyāvyākatacittasamaṅgissa cittaṃ jānāti.
     Ākāsānañcāyatanakiriyaṃ viññāṇañcāyatanakiriyassa āram-
maṇapaccayena paccayo. Ākiñcaññāyatanakiriyaṃ nevasañ-
ñā-nāsaññāyatanakiriyassa ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     Rūpāyatanaṃ cakkhuviññāṇassa ārammaṇapaccayena pac-
cayo. Saddāyatanaṃ cetoviññāṇassa, gandhāyatanaṃ ghā-
naviññāṇassa; rasāyatanaṃ jivhāviññāṇassa, phoṭṭhabbāya-
tanaṃ kāyaviññāṇassa ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     Avyākatā khandhā iddhividhañāṇassa cetopariyañāṇassa
pubbenivāsānussatiñāṇassa anāgataṃsañāṇassa āvajjanāya
ārammaṇapacceyan paccayo.
     Avyākato . . . kusalassa . . . ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.

     Sekhā phalaṃ paccavekkhanti nibbānaṃ paccavekkhanti.
Nibbānaṃ gotrabhussa vodānassa dhammassa ārammaṇa-
paccayena paccayo.
     Sekhā vā puthujjanā vā cakkhuṃ aniccato dukkhato anat-
tato vipassanti, sotaṃ ghānaṃ . . . rūpe . . . sadde . . .

ñāṇana vipākāvyākata-kiriyāvyākata-cittasamaṅgissa cittaṃ
jānanti.
     Avyākatā khandhā iddhividhañāṇassa cetopariyañāṇassa
pubbenivāsānussatiñāṇassa anāgataṃsañāṇassa ārammaṇa-
paccayena paccayo.
     Ayvākato . . . akusalassa . . . ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo
     Cakkhuṃ assādeti abhinandati; taṃ ārabbha rāgo uppajja-
ti, diṭṭhi . . . vicikicchā . . . uddhaccaṃ . . . domanassaṃ
uppajjati. Sotaṃ . . . ghānaṃ . . . rūpe . . . phoṭṭhabbe
vatthuṃ . . .
     Vipākāvyākate kiriyāvyākate khandhe assādeti abhinan-
dati, taṃ ārabbha rāgo uppajjati, diṭṭhi . . . vicikicchā . . .
uddhaccaṃ . . . domanassaṃ uppajjati.
                               3.
     Kusalo dhammo kusalassa . . . adhipati p.1 paccayo.
     (a) Ārammaṇādhipati, (b) Sahajātādhipati.
     (a) Ārammaṇādhipati:-- dānaṃ datvā, sīlaṃ samādiyitvā
uposathakammaṃ katvā taṃ garuṃ katvā paccavekkhati,
pubbe suciṇṇāni garuṃ katvā paccavekkhati, jhānā vuṭṭha-
hitvā jhānaṃ garuṃ katvā paccavekkhati; sekhā gotrabhuṃ
garuṃ katvā paccavekkhanti, vodānaṃ paccavekkhanti;
sekhā maggā vuṭṭhahitvā maggaṃ garuṃ katvā paccavek-
khanti.
     (b) Sahajātādhipati :-- kusalādhipati sampayuttakānaṃ
khandhānaṃ adhipatipaccayena paccayo.
     Kusalo dhammo akusalassa . . . adhipatip. paccayo.

     Kusalo dhammo kusalassa anantarap. paccayo.

ñā-nāsaññāyatanakusalaṃ phalasamāpattiyā anantarapacca-
yena paccayo.

mānaṃ akusalānaṃ khandhānaṃ anantarapaccayena paccayo.

     Akusalaṃ vuṭṭhānassa anantarapaccayena paccayo.

pacchimānaṃ pacchimānaṃ vipākāvyākatānaṃ kiriyāvyāka-
tānaṃ khandhānaṃ anantarapaccayena paccayo.
     Bhavaṅgaṃ āvajjanāya, kiriyaṃ vuṭṭhānassa, arahato

cayena paccayo.

                               9.
     Kusalo1 dhammo kusalassa dhammassa upanissayapacca-

     (a) Ārammaṇūpanissayo, (b) anantarūpanissayo, (c) pa-
katūpanissayo.
     (a) Dānaṃ datvā, sīlaṃ samādiyitvā, uposathakammaṃ
katvā, taṃ garuṃ katvā paccavekkhati; pubbe suciññāni
garuṃ katvā paccavekkhati; jhānā vuṭṭhahitvā, jhānaṃ garuṃ
katvā paccavekkhati; sekhā gotrabhuṃ garuṃ katvā paccavek-
khanti; vodānaṃ garuṃ katvā paccavekkhanti; sekhā maggā
vuṭṭhahitvā, maggaṃ garuṃ katvā paccavekkhanti.
     (b) Purimā purimā kusalā khandhā pacchimānaṃ pacchimā-
naṃ kusalānaṃ khandhānaṃ upanissayapaccayena paccayo.
Anulomaṃ gotrabhussa, anulomaṃ vodānassa, gotrabhu mag-
gassa, vodānaṃ maggassa upanissayapaccayena paccayo.
     (c) Saddhaṃ upanissāya, dānaṃ deti, sīlaṃ samādiyati, upo-
sathakammaṃ karoti: jhānaṃ uppādeti, vipassanaṃ . . .
maggaṃ . . . abhiññaṃ . . . samāpattiṃ uppādeti.
     Sīlaṃ, sutaṃ, cāgaṃ, paññaṃ upanissāya dānaṃ deti, sīlaṃ
samādiyati . . . (as above). Saddhā, sīlaṃ, sutaṃ, cāgo,
paññā saddhāya, sīlassa, sutassa, cāgassa, paññāya upanis-
sayapaccayena paccayo.
     Paṭhamassa jhānassa parikammaṃ paṭhamassa jhānassa
upanissayapaccayena paccayo; dutiyassa jhānassa parikam-
maṃ dutiyassa jhānassa upanissayapaccayena paccayo; . . .
(so for tatiyaṃ and catutthaṃ jhānaṃ).

     (a) Ārammaṇapurejātaṃ, (b) vatthupurejātaṃ.

. . . phoṭṭhabbāyatanaṃ kāyaviññāṇassa purejātapaccayena
paccayo.
     (b) Cakkhāyatanaṃ cakkhuviññāṇassa . . . sotāyatanaṃ

tapaccayena paccayo. Vatthu vipakāvyākatānaṃ kiriyā-
vyākatānaṃ khandhānaṃ purejātapaccayena paccayo.

anattato vipassanti. Sotaṃ . . . rūpe . . . vatthu aniccato
dukkhato anattato vipassanti, dibbena cakkhunā rūpaṃ

     (b) Vatthu kusalānaṃ khandhānaṃ purejātapaccayena pac-
cayo.
     Avyākato dhammo akusalassa . . . purejātap. paccayo.
     (a, b):-- (a) Cakkhuṃ assādeti abhinandati; taṃ ārabbha

     Kusalo dhammo kusalassa kammap. paccayo.
     Kusalā cetanā sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ kammapac-

     Kusalo dhammo avyākatassa . . . kammap. paccayo.
     (a) Sahajātā, (b) nānākhaṇikā.
     (a) Kusalā cetanā cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ kamma-
paccayena paccayo.
     (b) Nānākhaṇikā kusalā cetanā vipākānaṃ khandhānaṃ

     Kusalo dhammo kusalassa ca avyākatassa ca dhammassa
kammapaccayena paccayo.
     Kusalā cetanā sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasam-
uṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ kamma . . .

     Akusalo dhammo akusalassa . . . kammap. paccayo.
     Akusalā cetanā sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ kamma . . .
     Akusalo dhammo avyākatassa . . . kammap. paccayo.

     (b) Akusalā cetanā vipākānaṃ khandhānaṃ kaṭattā ca

     Avyākato dhammo avyākatassa . . . kammap. paccayo.
     Vipākāvyākatā kiriyāvyākatā cetanā sampayuttakānaṃ
khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ kamma . . .
Paṭisandhikkhaṇe vipākāvyākatā cetanā sampayuttakānaṃ

thussa kammapaccayena paccayo.
                               14.
     Avyākato dhammo avyākatassa . . . vipākap. paccayo.

cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ, dve khandhā dvinnaṃ
khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ vipākapaccayena
paccayo. Paṭisandhikkhaṇe vipākāvyākato eko khandho
tiṇṇaṃ khandhānaṃ kaṭattā ca rūpānaṃ, tayo khandhā . . .
dve khandhā dvinaṃ khandhānaṃ kaṭattā ca rūpānaṃ
vipāka . . . Khandhā vatthussa vipākapaccayena paccayo.

jata-paccayena paccayo.

spond to (a)-(d) above, substituting kusalo for akusalo and v.v.).
